<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dazzle.html>dazzle</a></strong> (<i>countable <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">dazzles</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>A</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:light.html>light</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> dazzling brilliancy.</li>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:psychology.html>psychology</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mildly mentally <a href = vnd.unilang:disabled.html>disabled</a> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">formally, <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:an.html>an</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:iq.html>Iq</a> ranging <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> 50 <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> 80</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">deech</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*dēg</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*daigaz</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dʰeyǵʰ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:build.html>build</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:mold.html>mold</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:form.html>form</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:knead.html>knead</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:deeg.html>deeg</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:deegje.html>deegje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
